    33	using rocksdb::Slice;
    34	
    35	bool MetadataFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, const Slice &value,
    36	                            [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
    37	  Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
    38	  rocksdb::Status s = metadata.Decode(value);
    39	  auto [ns, user_key] = ExtractNamespaceKey(key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    40	  if (!s.ok()) {
    41	    warn("[compact_filter/metadata] Failed to decode, namespace: {}, key: {}, err: {}", ns, user_key, s.ToString());
    42	    return false;
    43	  }
    44	  debug("[compact_filter/metadata] namespace: {}, key: {}, result: {}", ns, user_key,
    45	        (metadata.Expired() ? "deleted" : "reserved"));
    46	  return metadata.Expired();
    47	}
    48	
    49	Status SubKeyFilter::GetMetadata(const InternalKey &ikey, Metadata *metadata) const {
    50	  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
    51	  const auto cf_handles = stor_->GetCFHandles();
    52	  // storage close the would delete the column family handler and DB
    53	  if (!db || cf_handles->size() < 2) return {Status::NotOK, "storage is closed"};
    54	  std::string metadata_key = ComposeNamespaceKey(ikey.GetNamespace(), ikey.GetKey(), stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    55	
    56	  if (cached_key_.empty() || metadata_key != cached_key_) {
    57	    std::string bytes;
    58	    rocksdb::Status s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[1], metadata_key, &bytes);
    59	    cached_key_ = std::move(metadata_key);
    60	    if (s.ok()) {
    61	      cached_metadata_ = std::move(bytes);
    62	    } else if (s.IsNotFound()) {
    63	      // metadata was deleted(perhaps compaction or manual)
    64	      // clear the metadata
    65	      cached_metadata_.clear();
    66	      return {Status::NotFound, "metadata is not found"};
    67	    } else {
    68	      cached_key_.clear();
    69	      cached_metadata_.clear();
    70	      return {Status::NotOK, "fetch error: " + s.ToString()};
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	  // the metadata was not found
    74	  if (cached_metadata_.empty()) return {Status::NotFound, "metadata is not found"};
    75	  // the metadata is cached
    76	  rocksdb::Status s = metadata->Decode(cached_metadata_);
    77	  if (!s.ok()) {
    78	    cached_key_.clear();
    79	    return {Status::NotOK, "decode error: " + s.ToString()};
    80	  }
    81	  return Status::OK();
    82	}
    83	
    84	bool SubKeyFilter::IsMetadataExpired(const InternalKey &ikey, const Metadata &metadata) {
    85	  // lazy delete to avoid race condition between command Expire and subkey Compaction
    86	  // Related issue:https://github.com/apache/kvrocks/issues/1298
    87	  //
    88	  // `util::GetTimeStampMS() - 300000` means extending 5 minutes for expired items,
    89	  // to prevent them from being recycled once they reach the expiration time.
    90	  uint64_t lazy_expired_ts = util::GetTimeStampMS() - 300000;
    91	  return metadata.IsSingleKVType()  // metadata key was overwrite by set command
    92	         || metadata.ExpireAt(lazy_expired_ts) || ikey.GetVersion() != metadata.version;
    93	}
    94	
    95	rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision SubKeyFilter::FilterBlobByKey([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key,
    96	                                                                  [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value,
    97	                                                                  [[maybe_unused]] std::string *skip_until) const {
    98	  InternalKey ikey(key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    99	  Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
   100	  Status s = GetMetadata(ikey, &metadata);
   101	  if (s.Is<Status::NotFound>()) {
   102	    return rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kRemove;
   103	  }
   104	  if (!s.IsOK()) {
   105	    error("[compact_filter/subkey] Failed to get metadata, namespace: {}, key: {}, err: {}", ikey.GetNamespace(),
   106	          ikey.GetKey(), s.Msg());
   107	    return rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kKeep;
   108	  }
   109	  // bitmap will be checked in Filter
   110	  if (metadata.Type() == kRedisBitmap) {
   111	    return rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kUndetermined;
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  bool result = IsMetadataExpired(ikey, metadata);
   115	  return result ? rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kRemove : rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kKeep;
   116	}
   117	
   118	bool SubKeyFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, const Slice &value,
   119	                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
   120	  InternalKey ikey(key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
   121	  Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
   122	  Status s = GetMetadata(ikey, &metadata);
   123	  if (s.Is<Status::NotFound>()) {
   124	    return true;
   125	  }
   126	  if (!s.IsOK()) {
   127	    error("[compact_filter/subkey] Failed to get metadata, namespace: {}, key: {}, err: {}", ikey.GetNamespace(),
   128	          ikey.GetKey(), s.Msg());
   129	    return false;
   130	  }
   131	
   132	  return IsMetadataExpired(ikey, metadata) || (metadata.Type() == kRedisBitmap && redis::Bitmap::IsEmptySegment(value));
   133	}
   134	
   135	}  // namespace engine

    21	#pragma once

    28	namespace redis {

    30	enum class IndexOnDataType : uint8_t {
    31	  HASH = kRedisHash,
    32	  JSON = kRedisJson,
    33	};
    34	
    35	inline constexpr auto kErrorInsufficientLength = "insufficient length while decoding metadata";
    36	inline constexpr auto kErrorIncorrectLength = "length is too short or too long to be parsed as a vector";
    37	
    38	class IndexMetadata {
    39	 public:
    40	  uint8_t flag = 0;  // all reserved
    41	  IndexOnDataType on_data_type;
    42	
    43	  std::string_view OnDataTypeName() const { return RedisTypeNames[(size_t)on_data_type]; }
    44	
    45	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const {
    46	    PutFixed8(dst, flag);
    47	    PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(on_data_type));
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) {
    51	    if (!GetFixed8(input, &flag)) {
    52	      return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrorInsufficientLength);
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    if (!GetFixed8(input, reinterpret_cast<uint8_t *>(&on_data_type))) {
    56	      return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrorInsufficientLength);
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
    60	  }
    61	};
    62

    66	  PREFIXES = 1,

    68	  // field metadata
    69	  FIELD_META = 2,
    70

    90	inline const char *VectorTypeToString(VectorType type) {
    91	  switch (type) {
    92	    case VectorType::FLOAT64:
    93	      return "FLOAT64";
    94	  }
    95	
    96	  return "unknown";
    97	}

   106	  switch (dm) {
   107	    case DistanceMetric::L2:
   108	      return "L2";
   109	    case DistanceMetric::IP:
   110	      return "IP";
   111	    case DistanceMetric::COSINE:
   112	      return "COSINE";

   123	struct SearchKey {
   124	  std::string_view ns;
   125	  std::string_view index;
   126	  std::string_view field;
   127	
   128	  SearchKey(std::string_view ns, std::string_view index) : ns(ns), index(index) {}
   129	  SearchKey(std::string_view ns, std::string_view index, std::string_view field) : ns(ns), index(index), field(field) {}
   130	
   131	  void PutNamespace(std::string *dst) const {
   132	    PutFixed8(dst, ns.size());
   133	    dst->append(ns);
   134	  }
   135	
   136	  static void PutType(std::string *dst, SearchSubkeyType type) { PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(type)); }
   137	
   138	  void PutIndex(std::string *dst) const { PutSizedString(dst, index); }
   139	
   140	  static void PutHnswLevelType(std::string *dst, HnswLevelType type) { PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(type)); }
   141	
   142	  void PutHnswLevelPrefix(std::string *dst, uint16_t level) const {
   143	    PutNamespace(dst);
   144	    PutType(dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
   145	    PutIndex(dst);
   146	    PutSizedString(dst, field);
   147	    PutFixed16(dst, level);
   148	  }
   149	
   150	  void PutHnswLevelNodePrefix(std::string *dst, uint16_t level) const {
   151	    PutHnswLevelPrefix(dst, level);
   152	    PutHnswLevelType(dst, HnswLevelType::NODE);
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  void PutHnswLevelEdgePrefix(std::string *dst, uint16_t level) const {
   156	    PutHnswLevelPrefix(dst, level);
   157	    PutHnswLevelType(dst, HnswLevelType::EDGE);
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  std::string ConstructIndexMeta() const {
   161	    std::string dst;
   162	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   163	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META);
   164	    PutIndex(&dst);
   165	    return dst;
   166	  }
   167	
   168	  std::string ConstructIndexPrefixes() const {
   169	    std::string dst;
   170	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   171	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::PREFIXES);
   172	    PutIndex(&dst);
   173	    return dst;
   174	  }
   175	
   176	  std::string ConstructFieldMeta() const {
   177	    std::string dst;
   178	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   179	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_META);
   180	    PutIndex(&dst);
   181	    PutSizedString(&dst, field);
   182	    return dst;
   183	  }
   184	
   185	  std::string ConstructAllFieldMetaBegin() const {
   186	    std::string dst;
   187	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   188	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_META);
   189	    PutIndex(&dst);
   190	    PutFixed32(&dst, 0);
   191	    return dst;
   192	  }
   193	
   194	  std::string ConstructAllFieldMetaEnd() const {
   195	    std::string dst;
   196	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   197	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_META);
   198	    PutIndex(&dst);
   199	    PutFixed32(&dst, (uint32_t)(-1));
   200	    return dst;
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  std::string ConstructAllFieldDataBegin() const {
   204	    std::string dst;
   205	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   206	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
   207	    PutIndex(&dst);
   208	    PutFixed32(&dst, 0);
   209	    return dst;
   210	  }
   211	
   212	  std::string ConstructAllFieldDataEnd() const {
   213	    std::string dst;
   214	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   215	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
   216	    PutIndex(&dst);
   217	    PutFixed32(&dst, (uint32_t)(-1));
   218	    return dst;
   219	  }
   220	
   221	  std::string ConstructTagFieldData(std::string_view tag, std::string_view key) const {
   222	    std::string dst;
   223	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   224	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
   225	    PutIndex(&dst);
   226	    PutSizedString(&dst, field);
   227	    PutSizedString(&dst, tag);
   228	    PutSizedString(&dst, key);
   229	    return dst;
   230	  }
   231	
   232	  std::string ConstructNumericFieldData(double num, std::string_view key) const {
   233	    std::string dst;
   234	    PutNamespace(&dst);
   235	    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
   236	    PutIndex(&dst);
   237	    PutSizedString(&dst, field);
   238	    PutDouble(&dst, num);
   239	    PutSizedString(&dst, key);
   240	    return dst;
   241	  }
   242	
   243	  std::string ConstructHnswLevelNodePrefix(uint16_t level) const {
   244	    std::string dst;
   245	    PutHnswLevelNodePrefix(&dst, level);
   246	    return dst;
   247	  }
   248	
   249	  std::string ConstructHnswNode(uint16_t level, std::string_view key) const {
   250	    std::string dst;
   251	    PutHnswLevelNodePrefix(&dst, level);
   252	    PutSizedString(&dst, key);
   253	    return dst;
   254	  }
   255	
   256	  std::string ConstructHnswEdgeWithSingleEnd(uint16_t level, std::string_view key) const {
   257	    std::string dst;
   258	    PutHnswLevelEdgePrefix(&dst, level);
   259	    PutSizedString(&dst, key);
   260	    return dst;
   261	  }
   262	
   263	  std::string ConstructHnswEdge(uint16_t level, std::string_view key1, std::string_view key2) const {
   264	    std::string dst;
   265	    PutHnswLevelEdgePrefix(&dst, level);
   266	    PutSizedString(&dst, key1);
   267	    PutSizedString(&dst, key2);
   268	    return dst;
   269	  }
   270	};
   271	
   272	struct IndexPrefixes {
   273	  std::vector<std::string> prefixes;
   274	
   275	  static inline const std::string all[] = {""};
   276	
   277	  auto begin() const {  // NOLINT
   278	    return prefixes.empty() ? std::begin(all) : prefixes.data();
   279	  }
   280	
   281	  auto end() const {  // NOLINT
   282	    return prefixes.empty() ? std::end(all) : prefixes.data() + prefixes.size();
   283	  }
   284	
   285	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const {
   286	    for (const auto &prefix : prefixes) {
   287	      PutFixed32(dst, prefix.size());
   288	      dst->append(prefix);
   289	    }
   290	  }
   291	
   292	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) {
   293	    uint32_t size = 0;
   294	
   295	    while (GetFixed32(input, &size)) {
   296	      if (input->size() < size) return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   297	      prefixes.emplace_back(input->data(), size);
   298	      input->remove_prefix(size);
   299	    }
   300	
   301	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   302	  }
   303	};
   304	
   305	struct IndexFieldMetadata {
   306	  bool noindex = false;
   307	  IndexFieldType type;
   308	
   309	  explicit IndexFieldMetadata(IndexFieldType type) : type(type) {}
   310	
   311	  // flag: <noindex: 1 bit> <type: 4 bit> <reserved: 3 bit>
   312	  uint8_t MakeFlag() const { return noindex | (uint8_t)type << 1; }
   313	
   314	  void DecodeFlag(uint8_t flag) {
   315	    noindex = flag & 1;
   316	    type = DecodeType(flag);
   317	  }
   318	
   319	  static IndexFieldType DecodeType(uint8_t flag) { return IndexFieldType(flag >> 1); }
   320	
   321	  virtual ~IndexFieldMetadata() = default;
   322	
   323	  std::string_view Type() const {
   324	    switch (type) {
   325	      case IndexFieldType::TAG:
   326	        return "tag";
   327	      case IndexFieldType::NUMERIC:
   328	        return "numeric";
   329	      case IndexFieldType::VECTOR:
   330	        return "vector";
   331	      default:
   332	        return "unknown";
   333	    }
   334	  }
   335	
   336	  virtual void Encode(std::string *dst) const { PutFixed8(dst, MakeFlag()); }
   337	
   338	  virtual rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) {
   339	    uint8_t flag = 0;
   340	    if (!GetFixed8(input, &flag)) {
   341	      return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   342	    }
   343	
   344	    DecodeFlag(flag);
   345	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   346	  }
   347	
   348	  virtual bool IsSortable() const { return false; }
   349	
   350	  static inline rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input, std::unique_ptr<IndexFieldMetadata> &ptr);
   351	};
   352	
   353	struct TagFieldMetadata : IndexFieldMetadata {
   354	  char separator = ',';
   355	  bool case_sensitive = false;
   356	
   357	  TagFieldMetadata() : IndexFieldMetadata(IndexFieldType::TAG) {}
   358	
   359	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const override {
   360	    IndexFieldMetadata::Encode(dst);
   361	    PutFixed8(dst, separator);
   362	    PutFixed8(dst, case_sensitive);
   363	  }
   364	
   365	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) override {
   366	    if (auto s = IndexFieldMetadata::Decode(input); !s.ok()) {
   367	      return s;
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    if (input->size() < 2) {
   371	      return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   372	    }
   373	
   374	    GetFixed8(input, (uint8_t *)&separator);
   375	    GetFixed8(input, (uint8_t *)&case_sensitive);
   376	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   377	  }
   378	};
   379	
   380	struct NumericFieldMetadata : IndexFieldMetadata {
   381	  NumericFieldMetadata() : IndexFieldMetadata(IndexFieldType::NUMERIC) {}
   382	
   383	  bool IsSortable() const override { return true; }
   384	};
   385	
   386	struct HnswVectorFieldMetadata : IndexFieldMetadata {
   387	  VectorType vector_type;
   388	  uint16_t dim;
   389	  DistanceMetric distance_metric;
   390	
   391	  uint32_t initial_cap = 500000;   // Initial vector capacity
   392	  uint16_t m = 16;                 // Max allowed outgoing edges per node
   393	  uint32_t ef_construction = 200;  // Max potential outgoing edge candidates during construction
   394	  uint32_t ef_runtime = 10;        // Max top candidates held during KNN search
   395	  double epsilon = 0.01;           // Relative factor setting search boundaries in range queries
   396	  uint16_t num_levels = 0;         // Number of levels in the HNSW graph
   397	
   398	  HnswVectorFieldMetadata() : IndexFieldMetadata(IndexFieldType::VECTOR) {}
   399	
   400	  bool IsSortable() const override { return true; }
   401	
   402	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const override {
   403	    IndexFieldMetadata::Encode(dst);
   404	    PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(vector_type));
   405	    PutFixed16(dst, dim);
   406	    PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(distance_metric));
   407	    PutFixed32(dst, initial_cap);
   408	    PutFixed16(dst, m);
   409	    PutFixed32(dst, ef_construction);
   410	    PutFixed32(dst, ef_runtime);
   411	    PutDouble(dst, epsilon);
   412	    PutFixed16(dst, num_levels);
   413	  }
   414	
   415	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) override {
   416	    if (auto s = IndexFieldMetadata::Decode(input); !s.ok()) {
   417	      return s;
   418	    }
   419	
   420	    constexpr size_t required_size = sizeof(uint8_t) + sizeof(uint16_t) + sizeof(uint8_t) + sizeof(uint32_t) +
   421	                                     sizeof(uint16_t) + sizeof(uint32_t) + sizeof(uint32_t) + sizeof(uint64_t) +
   422	                                     sizeof(uint16_t);
   423	
   424	    if (input->size() < required_size) {
   425	      return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   426	    }
   427	
   428	    GetFixed8(input, (uint8_t *)(&vector_type));
   429	    GetFixed16(input, &dim);
   430	    GetFixed8(input, (uint8_t *)(&distance_metric));
   431	    GetFixed32(input, &initial_cap);
   432	    GetFixed16(input, &m);
   433	    GetFixed32(input, &ef_construction);
   434	    GetFixed32(input, &ef_runtime);
   435	    GetDouble(input, &epsilon);
   436	    GetFixed16(input, &num_levels);
   437	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   438	  }
   439	};
   440	
   441	struct HnswNodeFieldMetadata {
   442	  uint16_t num_neighbours;
   443	  std::vector<double> vector;
   444	
   445	  HnswNodeFieldMetadata() = default;
   446	  HnswNodeFieldMetadata(uint16_t num_neighbours, std::vector<double> vector)
   447	      : num_neighbours(num_neighbours), vector(std::move(vector)) {}
   448	
   449	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const {
   450	    PutFixed16(dst, num_neighbours);
   451	    PutFixed16(dst, static_cast<uint16_t>(vector.size()));
   452	    for (double element : vector) {
   453	      PutDouble(dst, element);
   454	    }
   455	  }
   456	
   457	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) {
   458	    if (input->size() < 2 + 2) {
   459	      return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   460	    }
   461	    GetFixed16(input, (uint16_t *)(&num_neighbours));
   462	
   463	    uint16_t dim = 0;
   464	    GetFixed16(input, (uint16_t *)(&dim));
   465	
   466	    if (input->size() != dim * sizeof(double)) {
   467	      return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorIncorrectLength);
   468	    }
   469	    vector.resize(dim);
   470	
   471	    for (auto i = 0; i < dim; ++i) {
   472	      GetDouble(input, &vector[i]);
   473	    }
   474	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   475	  }
   476	};
   477	
   478	inline rocksdb::Status IndexFieldMetadata::Decode(Slice *input, std::unique_ptr<IndexFieldMetadata> &ptr) {
   479	  if (input->size() < 1) {
   480	    return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   481	  }
   482	
   483	  switch (DecodeType((*input)[0])) {
   484	    case IndexFieldType::TAG:
   485	      ptr = std::make_unique<TagFieldMetadata>();
   486	      break;
   487	    case IndexFieldType::NUMERIC:
   488	      ptr = std::make_unique<NumericFieldMetadata>();
   489	      break;
   490	    case IndexFieldType::VECTOR:
   491	      ptr = std::make_unique<HnswVectorFieldMetadata>();
   492	      break;
   493	    default:
   494	      return rocksdb::Status::Corruption("encountered unknown field type");
   495	  }
   496	
   497	  return ptr->Decode(input);
   498	}
   499	
   500	}  // namespace redis

    30	TEST(Compact, Filter) {
    31	  Config config;
    32	  config.db_dir = "compactdb";
    33	  config.slot_id_encoded = false;
    34	
    35	  auto storage = std::make_unique<engine::Storage>(&config);
    36	  Status s = storage->Open();
    37	  assert(s.IsOK());
    38	
    39	  uint64_t ret = 0;
    40	  std::string ns = "test_compact";
    41	  auto hash = std::make_unique<redis::Hash>(storage.get(), ns);
    42	  std::string expired_hash_key = "expire_hash_key";
    43	  std::string live_hash_key = "live_hash_key";
    44	
    45	  engine::Context ctx(storage.get());
    46	
    47	  hash->Set(ctx, expired_hash_key, "f1", "v1", &ret);
    48	  hash->Set(ctx, expired_hash_key, "f2", "v2", &ret);
    49	  auto st = hash->Expire(ctx, expired_hash_key, 1);  // expired
    50	  usleep(10000);
    51	  hash->Set(ctx, live_hash_key, "f1", "v1", &ret);
    52	  hash->Set(ctx, live_hash_key, "f2", "v2", &ret);
    53	
    54	  auto status = storage->Compact(nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);
    55	  assert(status.ok());
    56	  // Compact twice to workaround issue fixed by: https://github.com/facebook/rocksdb/pull/11468
    57	  status = storage->Compact(nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);
    58	  assert(status.ok());
    59	
    60	  rocksdb::DB* db = storage->GetDB();
    61	  rocksdb::ReadOptions read_options;
    62	  read_options.snapshot = db->GetSnapshot();
    63	  read_options.fill_cache = false;
    64	
    65	  auto new_iterator = [db, read_options, &storage](ColumnFamilyID column_family_id) {
    66	    return std::unique_ptr<rocksdb::Iterator>(db->NewIterator(read_options, storage->GetCFHandle(column_family_id)));
    67	  };
    68	
    69	  auto iter = new_iterator(ColumnFamilyID::Metadata);
    70	  for (iter->SeekToFirst(); iter->Valid(); iter->Next()) {
    71	    auto [user_ns, user_key] = ExtractNamespaceKey(iter->key(), storage->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    72	    EXPECT_EQ(user_key.ToString(), live_hash_key);
    73	  }
    74	
    75	  iter = new_iterator(ColumnFamilyID::PrimarySubkey);
    76	  for (iter->SeekToFirst(); iter->Valid(); iter->Next()) {
    77	    InternalKey ikey(iter->key(), storage->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    78	    EXPECT_EQ(ikey.GetKey().ToString(), live_hash_key);
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  auto zset = std::make_unique<redis::ZSet>(storage.get(), ns);
    82	  std::string expired_zset_key = "expire_zset_key";
    83	  std::vector<MemberScore> member_scores = {MemberScore{"z1", 1.1}, MemberScore{"z2", 0.4}};
    84	  zset->Add(ctx, expired_zset_key, ZAddFlags::Default(), &member_scores, &ret);
    85	  st = zset->Expire(ctx, expired_zset_key, 1);  // expired
    86	  usleep(10000);
    87	
    88	  // Same as the above compact, need to compact twice here
    89	  status = storage->Compact(nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);
    90	  EXPECT_TRUE(status.ok());
    91	  status = storage->Compact(nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);
    92	  EXPECT_TRUE(status.ok());
    93	
    94	  iter = new_iterator(ColumnFamilyID::PrimarySubkey);
    95	  for (iter->SeekToFirst(); iter->Valid(); iter->Next()) {
    96	    InternalKey ikey(iter->key(), storage->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    97	    EXPECT_EQ(ikey.GetKey().ToString(), live_hash_key);
    98	  }
    99	
   100	  iter = new_iterator(ColumnFamilyID::SecondarySubkey);
   101	  for (iter->SeekToFirst(); iter->Valid(); iter->Next()) {
   102	    EXPECT_TRUE(false);  // never reach here
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  Slice mk_with_ttl = "mk_with_ttl";
   106	  hash->Set(ctx, mk_with_ttl, "f1", "v1", &ret);
   107	  hash->Set(ctx, mk_with_ttl, "f2", "v2", &ret);
   108	
   109	  int retry = 2;
   110	  while (retry-- > 0) {
   111	    status = storage->Compact(nullptr, nullptr, nullptr);
   112	    ASSERT_TRUE(status.ok());
   113	    std::vector<FieldValue> fieldvalues;
   114	    auto get_res = hash->GetAll(ctx, mk_with_ttl, &fieldvalues);
   115	    auto s_expire = hash->Expire(ctx, mk_with_ttl, 1);  // expired immediately..
   116	
   117	    if (retry == 1) {
   118	      ASSERT_TRUE(get_res.ok());  // not expired first time
   119	      ASSERT_TRUE(s_expire.ok());

   121	      ASSERT_TRUE(get_res.ok());  // expired but still return ok....
   122	      ASSERT_EQ(0, fieldvalues.size());
   123	      ASSERT_TRUE(s_expire.IsNotFound());
   124	    }
   125	    usleep(10000);
   126	  }

   132	    std::cout << "Encounter filesystem error: " << ec << std::endl;
   133	  }

    41	namespace redis {
    42	
    43	struct GlobalIndexer;
    44	
    45	struct FieldValueRetriever {
    46	  struct HashData {
    47	    Hash hash;
    48	    HashMetadata metadata;
    49	    std::string_view key;
    50	
    51	    HashData(Hash hash, HashMetadata metadata, std::string_view key)
    52	        : hash(std::move(hash)), metadata(std::move(metadata)), key(key) {}
    53	  };
    54	  using JsonData = JsonValue;
    55	
    56	  using Variant = std::variant<HashData, JsonData>;
    57	  Variant db;
    58	
    59	  static StatusOr<FieldValueRetriever> Create(IndexOnDataType type, std::string_view key, engine::Storage *storage,
    60	                                              const std::string &ns);
    61	
    62	  explicit FieldValueRetriever(Hash hash, HashMetadata metadata, std::string_view key)
    63	      : db(std::in_place_type<HashData>, std::move(hash), std::move(metadata), key) {}
    64	
    65	  explicit FieldValueRetriever(JsonValue json) : db(std::in_place_type<JsonData>, std::move(json)) {}
    66	
    67	  StatusOr<kqir::Value> Retrieve(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view field, const redis::IndexFieldMetadata *type);
    68	
    69	  static StatusOr<kqir::Value> ParseFromJson(const jsoncons::json &value, const redis::IndexFieldMetadata *type);
    70	  static StatusOr<kqir::Value> ParseFromHash(const std::string &value, const redis::IndexFieldMetadata *type);
    71	};
    72	
    73	struct IndexUpdater {
    74	  using FieldValues = std::map<std::string, kqir::Value>;
    75	
    76	  const kqir::IndexInfo *info = nullptr;
    77	  GlobalIndexer *indexer = nullptr;
    78	  std::mutex update_mutex;
    79	
    80	  explicit IndexUpdater(const kqir::IndexInfo *info) : info(info) {}
    81	
    82	  StatusOr<FieldValues> Record(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view key) const;
    83	  Status UpdateIndex(engine::Context &ctx, const std::string &field, std::string_view key, const kqir::Value &original,
    84	                     const kqir::Value &current);
    85	  Status Update(engine::Context &ctx, const FieldValues &original, std::string_view key);
    86	
    87	  Status Build(engine::Context &ctx);
    88	
    89	  Status UpdateTagIndex(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view key, const kqir::Value &original,
    90	                        const kqir::Value &current, const SearchKey &search_key, const TagFieldMetadata *tag) const;
    91	  Status UpdateNumericIndex(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view key, const kqir::Value &original,
    92	                            const kqir::Value &current, const SearchKey &search_key,
    93	                            const NumericFieldMetadata *num) const;
    94	  Status UpdateHnswVectorIndex(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view key, const kqir::Value &original,
    95	                               const kqir::Value &current, const SearchKey &search_key,
    96	                               HnswVectorFieldMetadata *vector);
    97	};
    98	
    99	struct GlobalIndexer {
   100	  using FieldValues = IndexUpdater::FieldValues;
   101	  struct RecordResult {
   102	    IndexUpdater *updater;
   103	    std::string key;
   104	    FieldValues fields;
   105	  };
   106	
   107	  tsl::htrie_map<char, IndexUpdater *> prefix_map;
   108	  std::vector<std::unique_ptr<IndexUpdater>> updater_list;
   109	
   110	  engine::Storage *storage = nullptr;
   111	
   112	  explicit GlobalIndexer(engine::Storage *storage) : storage(storage) {}
   113	
   114	  void Add(std::unique_ptr<IndexUpdater> updater);
   115	  void Remove(const kqir::IndexInfo *index);
   116	
   117	  StatusOr<RecordResult> Record(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view key, const std::string &ns);
   118	  static Status Update(engine::Context &ctx, const RecordResult &original);
   119	};
   120	
   121	}  // namespace redis

#include "db_util.h"

namespace redis {

StatusOr<FieldValueRetriever> FieldValueRetriever::Create(IndexOnDataType type, std::string_view key,
                                                          engine::Storage *storage, const std::string &ns) {
  engine::Context ctx(storage);
  if (type == IndexOnDataType::HASH) {
    Hash db(storage, ns);
    std::string ns_key = db.AppendNamespacePrefix(key);
    HashMetadata metadata(false);

    auto s = db.GetMetadata(ctx, ns_key, &metadata);
    if (!s.ok()) return {Status::NotOK, s.ToString()};
    return FieldValueRetriever(db, metadata, key);
  } else if (type == IndexOnDataType::JSON) {
    Json db(storage, ns);
    std::string ns_key = db.AppendNamespacePrefix(key);
    JsonMetadata metadata(false);
    JsonValue value;
    auto s = db.read(ctx, ns_key, &metadata, &value);
    if (!s.ok()) return {Status::NotOK, s.ToString()};
    return FieldValueRetriever(value);
  } else {
    unreachable();
  }
}

StatusOr<kqir::Value> FieldValueRetriever::ParseFromJson(const jsoncons::json &val,
                                                         const redis::IndexFieldMetadata *type) {
  if (auto numeric [[maybe_unused]] = dynamic_cast<const redis::NumericFieldMetadata *>(type)) {
    if (!val.is_number() || val.is_string()) return {Status::NotOK, "json value cannot be string for numeric fields"};
    return kqir::MakeValue<kqir::Numeric>(val.as_double());
  } else if (auto tag = dynamic_cast<const redis::TagFieldMetadata *>(type)) {
    if (val.is_string()) {
      const char delim[] = {tag->separator, '\0'};
--
}

StatusOr<kqir::Value> FieldValueRetriever::Retrieve(engine::Context &ctx, std::string_view field,
                                                    const redis::IndexFieldMetadata *type) {
  if (std::holds_alternative<HashData>(db)) {
    auto &[hash, metadata, key] = std::get<HashData>(db);
    std::string ns_key = hash.AppendNamespacePrefix(key);
    std::string sub_key = InternalKey(ns_key, field, metadata.version, hash.storage_->IsSlotIdEncoded()).Encode();
    std::string value;
    auto s = hash.storage_->Get(ctx, ctx.GetReadOptions(), sub_key, &value);
    if (s.IsNotFound()) return {Status::NotFound, s.ToString()};
    if (!s.ok()) return {Status::NotOK, s.ToString()};

    return ParseFromHash(value, type);
  } else if (std::holds_alternative<JsonData>(db)) {
    auto &value = std::get<JsonData>(db);

    auto s = value.Get(field.front() == '$' ? field : fmt::format("$.{}", field));
    if (!s.IsOK()) return {Status::NotOK, s.Msg()};
    if (s->value.size() != 1)
      return {Status::NotFound, "json value specified by the field (json path) should exist and be unique"};
    auto val = s->value[0];

--

  // key not exist

    // not the expected type, stop record
    return {Status::TypeMismatched};
  }

  std::string_view index;
  std::string_view field;

  SearchKey(std::string_view ns, std::string_view index) : ns(ns), index(index) {}
  SearchKey(std::string_view ns, std::string_view index, std::string_view field) : ns(ns), index(index), field(field) {}

  void PutNamespace(std::string *dst) const {
    PutFixed8(dst, ns.size());
    dst->append(ns);
  }

  static void PutType(std::string *dst, SearchSubkeyType type) { PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(type)); }

  void PutIndex(std::string *dst) const { PutSizedString(dst, index); }

  static void PutHnswLevelType(std::string *dst, HnswLevelType type) { PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(type)); }

  void PutHnswLevelPrefix(std::string *dst, uint16_t level) const {
    PutNamespace(dst);
    PutType(dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
    PutIndex(dst);
    PutSizedString(dst, field);
    PutFixed16(dst, level);
  }

  void PutHnswLevelNodePrefix(std::string *dst, uint16_t level) const {
    PutHnswLevelPrefix(dst, level);
    PutHnswLevelType(dst, HnswLevelType::NODE);
  }
--

  std::string ConstructIndexMeta() const {
    std::string dst;
    PutNamespace(&dst);
    PutType(&dst, SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META);
    PutIndex(&dst);
    return dst;
  }

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_search_compaction.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Test script to verify search compaction filter functionality.
This script will:
1. Build the project
2. Run the tests to verify search compaction filter works
"""

import subprocess
import sys
import os

def run_command(cmd, cwd=None):
    """Run a command and return its output"""
    print(f"Running: {cmd}")
    result = subprocess.run(
        cmd,
        shell=True,
        cwd=cwd,
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    if result.returncode != 0:
        print(f"Error running command: {cmd}")
        print(f"stdout: {result.stdout}")
        print(f"stderr: {result.stderr}")
        return False
    print(f"Success: {result.stdout}")
    return True

def main():
    testbed = "/testbed"
    build_dir = os.path.join(testbed, "build")
    
    # Build the project
    print("Building the project...")
    if not run_command("cmake --build . --parallel", cwd=build_dir):
        print("Build failed!")
        return 1
    
    # Run the compact test (includes search compaction filter tests)
    print("\nRunning compact tests...")
    test_exe = os.path.join(build_dir, "unittest")
    if not run_command(f"{test_exe} --gtest_filter=Compact.*", cwd=build_dir):
        print("Tests failed!")
        return 1
    
    print("\nAll tests passed!")
    return 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sys.exit(main())

inline bool GetSizedString(rocksdb::Slice *input, rocksdb::Slice *value) {
  uint32_t size = 0;
  if (!GetFixed32(input, &size)) return false;

  if (input->size() < size) return false;
  *value = rocksdb::Slice(input->data(), size);
  input->remove_prefix(size);
  return true;
}

bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
  // Parse the search key to extract namespace, type, and original key
  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
  const auto cf_handles = stor_->GetCFHandles();
  
  // storage closed would delete the column family handler and DB
  if (!db || cf_handles->size() < 2) return false;

  Slice input = key;
  
  // Extract namespace (1 byte size + data)
  uint8_t ns_size = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_size)) return false;
  if (input.size() < ns_size) return false;
  
  std::string ns(input.data(), ns_size);
  input.remove_prefix(ns_size);
  
  // Extract type (1 byte)
  uint8_t type_byte = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_byte)) return false;
  
  auto type = static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_byte);
  
  // Extract index name (4 bytes size + data)
  Slice index_name;
  if (!GetSizedString(&input, &index_name)) return false;
  
  // Handle different search subkey types
  switch (type) {
    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META:
    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::PREFIXES: {
      // These are metadata entries, we check if the index still exists
      // by checking if we can read the INDEX_META key
      std::string index_meta_key;
      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, index_name);
      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
      
      std::string index_meta_value;
      auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Search)],
                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
      
      // If this is the INDEX_META key itself, keep it
      if (type == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) {
        return false;
      }
      
      // For PREFIXES, delete if INDEX_META doesn'"'"'t exist
      return s.IsNotFound();
    }
    
    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_META: {
      // Field metadata - check if index exists
      std::string index_meta_key;
      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, index_name);
      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
      
      std::string index_meta_value;
      auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Search)],
                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
      
      return s.IsNotFound();
    }
    
    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD: {
      // Field data - extract the field name
      Slice field_name;
      if (!GetSizedString(&input, &field_name)) return false;
      
      // The remaining part contains field-specific data and the original key
      // For tag fields: tag (sized string) + key (sized string)
      // For numeric fields: number (8 bytes) + key (sized string)
      // For vector/hnsw fields: level info + key (sized string)
      
      // Try to extract the key - it'"'"'s typically at the end as a sized string
      // We need to find it by parsing field-specific data
      
      // For now, we'"'"'ll attempt to extract the last sized string as the key
      // This is a simplified approach that works for most field types
      
      // Skip field-specific data and try to get the key
      // The exact parsing depends on the field type, but we can try a heuristic:
      // - Look for a sized string that could be a valid key
      
      // For tag fields: skip tag, get key
      Slice potential_key;
      if (input.size() >= 4) {
        // Try to parse as tag field (tag + key)
        Slice tag;
        Slice remaining = input;
        if (GetSizedString(&remaining, &tag) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
          // Successfully parsed as tag field
        } else {
          // Try to parse as numeric field (double + key)
          remaining = input;
          double num;
          if (GetDouble(&remaining, &num) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
            // Successfully parsed as numeric field
          } else {
            // Try to parse as hnsw field (various structures)
            // For hnsw nodes/edges, the key is still at specific positions
            // This is complex, so for now we'"'"'ll be conservative
            return false;
          }
        }
        
        // Now check if the original key exists and is not expired
        std::string metadata_key = ComposeNamespaceKey(ns, potential_key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
        std::string metadata_bytes;
        auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Metadata)],
                         metadata_key, &metadata_bytes);
        
        if (s.IsNotFound()) {
          // Original key doesn'"'"'t exist, delete this search entry
          return true;
        }
        
        if (!s.ok()) {
          // Error reading metadata, keep the entry to be safe
          return false;
        }
        
        // Check if the key is expired
        Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
        rocksdb::Status decode_status = metadata.Decode(metadata_bytes);
        if (!decode_status.ok()) {
          // Failed to decode metadata, keep the entry to be safe
          return false;
        }
        
        // Delete if expired
        return metadata.Expired();
      }
      
      // Could not parse the key structure, keep it to be safe
      return false;
    }
    
    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_ALIAS: {
      // Field aliases - check if index exists
      std::string index_meta_key;
      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, index_name);
      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
      
      std::string index_meta_value;
      auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Search)],
                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
      
      return s.IsNotFound();
    }
    
    default:
      // Unknown type, keep it to be safe
      return false;
  }
}'

   137	bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
   138	                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
   139	  // Parse the search key to extract namespace, type, and original key
   140	  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
   141	  const auto cf_handles = stor_->GetCFHandles();
   142	  
   143	  // storage closed would delete the column family handler and DB
   144	  if (!db || cf_handles->size() < 2) return false;
   145	
   146	  Slice input = key;
   147	  
   148	  // Extract namespace (1 byte size + data)
   149	  uint8_t ns_size = 0;
   150	  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_size)) return false;
   151	  if (input.size() < ns_size) return false;
   152	  
   153	  std::string ns(input.data(), ns_size);
   154	  input.remove_prefix(ns_size);
   155	  
   156	  // Extract type (1 byte)
   157	  uint8_t type_byte = 0;
   158	  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_byte)) return false;
   159	  
   160	  auto type = static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_byte);
   161	  
   162	  // Extract index name (4 bytes size + data)
   163	  Slice index_name;
   164	  if (!GetSizedString(&input, &index_name)) return false;
   165	  
   166	  // Handle different search subkey types
   167	  switch (type) {
   168	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META:
   169	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::PREFIXES: {
   170	      // These are metadata entries, we check if the index still exists
   171	      // by checking if we can read the INDEX_META key
   172	      std::string index_meta_key;
   173	      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, index_name);
   174	      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
   175	      
   176	      std::string index_meta_value;
   177	      auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Search)],
   178	                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
   179	      
   180	      // If this is the INDEX_META key itself, keep it
   181	      if (type == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) {
   182	        return false;
   183	      }
   184	      
   185	      // For PREFIXES, delete if INDEX_META doesn't exist
   186	      return s.IsNotFound();
   187	    }
   188	    
   189	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_META: {
   190	      // Field metadata - check if index exists
   191	      std::string index_meta_key;
   192	      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, index_name);
   193	      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
   194

   197	                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
   198	      
   199	      return s.IsNotFound();
   200	    }
   201	    
   202	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD: {
   203	      // Field data - extract the field name
   204	      Slice field_name;
   205	      if (!GetSizedString(&input, &field_name)) return false;
   206	      
   207	      // The remaining part contains field-specific data and the original key
   208	      // For tag fields: tag (sized string) + key (sized string)
   209	      // For numeric fields: number (8 bytes) + key (sized string)
   210	      // For vector/hnsw fields: level info + key (sized string)
   211	      
   212	      // Try to extract the key - it's typically at the end as a sized string
   213	      // We need to find it by parsing field-specific data
   214	      
   215	      // For now, we'll attempt to extract the last sized string as the key
   216	      // This is a simplified approach that works for most field types
   217	      
   218	      // Skip field-specific data and try to get the key
   219	      // The exact parsing depends on the field type, but we can try a heuristic:
   220	      // - Look for a sized string that could be a valid key
   221	      
   222	      // For tag fields: skip tag, get key
   223	      Slice potential_key;
   224	      if (input.size() >= 4) {
   225	        // Try to parse as tag field (tag + key)
   226	        Slice tag;
   227	        Slice remaining = input;
   228	        if (GetSizedString(&remaining, &tag) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   229	          // Successfully parsed as tag field
   230	        } else {
   231	          // Try to parse as numeric field (double + key)
   232	          remaining = input;
   233	          double num;
   234	          if (GetDouble(&remaining, &num) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   235	            // Successfully parsed as numeric field
   236	          } else {

   241	          }
   242	        }

   253	        }

   258	        }

   263	        if (!decode_status.ok()) {
   264	          // Failed to decode metadata, keep the entry to be safe

   266	        }
   267

   270	      }
   271	      
   272	      // Could not parse the key structure, keep it to be safe

  std::string ConstructHnswNode(uint16_t level, std::string_view key) const {
    std::string dst;
    PutHnswLevelNodePrefix(&dst, level);
    PutSizedString(&dst, key);
    return dst;
  }

  std::string ConstructHnswEdgeWithSingleEnd(uint16_t level, std::string_view key) const {
    std::string dst;
    PutHnswLevelEdgePrefix(&dst, level);
    PutSizedString(&dst, key);
    return dst;
  }

  std::string ConstructHnswEdge(uint16_t level, std::string_view key1, std::string_view key2) const {
    std::string dst;
    PutHnswLevelEdgePrefix(&dst, level);
    PutSizedString(&dst, key1);
    PutSizedString(&dst, key2);
    return dst;
  }
};

struct IndexPrefixes {
  std::vector<std::string> prefixes;

  static inline const std::string all[] = {""};

  auto begin() const {  // NOLINT
    return prefixes.empty() ? std::begin(all) : prefixes.data();
  }

  auto end() const {  // NOLINT
    return prefixes.empty() ? std::end(all) : prefixes.data() + prefixes.size();
  }

  void PutIndex(std::string *dst) const { PutSizedString(dst, index); }

  void PutHnswLevelPrefix(std::string *dst, uint16_t level) const {
    PutNamespace(dst);
    PutType(dst, SearchSubkeyType::FIELD);
    PutIndex(dst);

I see! HNSW nodes have this structure:
- namespace (1 byte size + data)
- type (1 byte) = FIELD
- index name (sized string)
- field name (sized string)
- level (2 bytes)
- level type (1 byte) = NODE or EDGE
- key (sized string) [for nodes]
- key1, key2 (sized strings) [for edges]

Let me improve the implementation to handle HNSW keys properly:

      // For tag fields: tag (sized string) + key (sized string)
      // For numeric fields: number (8 bytes) + key (sized string)
      // For vector/hnsw fields: level info + key (sized string)

      // We need to find it by parsing field-specific data
      
      // For now, we'"'"'ll attempt to extract the last sized string as the key
      // This is a simplified approach that works for most field types

      // Field data - extract the field name
      Slice field_name;
      if (!GetSizedString(&input, &field_name)) return false;
      
      // The remaining part contains field-specific data and the original key
      // For tag fields: tag (sized string) + key (sized string)
      // For numeric fields: number (8 bytes) + key (sized string)
      // For vector/hnsw fields: level (2 bytes) + level_type (1 byte) + key (sized string)
      
      Slice potential_key;
      if (input.size() >= 4) {
        // Try to parse as tag field (tag + key)
        Slice tag;
        Slice remaining = input;
        if (GetSizedString(&remaining, &tag) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
          // Successfully parsed as tag field
        } else {
          // Try to parse as numeric field (double + key)
          remaining = input;
          double num;
          if (GetDouble(&remaining, &num) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
            // Successfully parsed as numeric field
          } else {
            // Try to parse as hnsw field
            // Structure: level (2 bytes) + level_type (1 byte) + key(s)
            remaining = input;
            uint16_t level;
            uint8_t level_type;
            if (input.size() >= 3 && GetFixed16(&remaining, &level) && GetFixed8(&remaining, &level_type)) {
              // Check the level type
              if (level_type == static_cast<uint8_t>(redis::HnswLevelType::NODE)) {
                // HNSW node: just one key
                if (!GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
                  // Could not parse, keep it to be safe
                  return false;
                }

                  // Could not parse, keep it to be safe
                  return false;

              } else {
                // Unknown level type, keep it to be safe
                return false;
              }

              // Could not parse any known field type, keep it to be safe
              return false;

        std::string metadata_bytes;

        if (s.IsNotFound()) {
          // Original key doesn'"'"'t exist, delete this search entry
          return true;

          // Error reading metadata, keep the entry to be safe
          return false;

    38	        ^
    39	        (?P<major>0|[1-9]\d*)
    40	        \.
    41	        (?P<minor>0|[1-9]\d*)

    58	# NOTE: the return type should be Popen[str], but Popen is not subscriptable before python 3.9
    59	def run(*args: str, msg: Optional[str] = None, verbose: bool = False, **kwargs: Any) -> Popen:
    60	    sys.stdout.flush()
    61	    if verbose:
    62	        print(f"$ {' '.join(args)}")
    63	
    64	    p = Popen(args, **kwargs)
    65	    code = p.wait()
    66	    if code != 0:
    67	        err = f"\nfailed to run: {args}\nexit with code: {code}\n"
    68	        if msg:
    69	            err += f"error message: {msg}\n"
    70	        raise RuntimeError(err)
    71	
    72	    return p
    73	
    74	
    75	def run_pipe(*args: str, msg: Optional[str] = None, verbose: bool = False, **kwargs: Any) -> IO[str]:
    76	    p = run(*args, msg=msg, verbose=verbose, stdout=PIPE, universal_newlines=True, **kwargs)
    77	    return p.stdout # type: ignore
    78	
    79	
    80	def find_command(command: str, msg: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
    81	    return run_pipe("which", command, msg=msg).read().strip()
    82	
    83	
    84	def check_version(current: str, required: Tuple[int, int, int], prog_name: Optional[str] = None) -> Tuple[
    85	    int, int, int]:
    86	    require_version = '.'.join(map(str, required))
    87	    semver_match = SEMVER_REGEX.match(current)
    88	    if semver_match is None:
    89	        raise RuntimeError(f"{prog_name} {require_version} or higher is required, got: {current}")
    90	    semver_dict = semver_match.groupdict()
    91	    semver = (int(semver_dict["major"]), int(semver_dict["minor"]), int(semver_dict["patch"]))
    92	    if semver < required:
    93	        raise RuntimeError(f"{prog_name} {require_version} or higher is required, got: {current}")
    94	
    95	    return semver
    96	
    97	def prepare() -> None:
    98	    basedir = Path(__file__).parent.absolute()
    99	    
   100	    # Install Git hooks
   101	    hooks = basedir / "dev" / "hooks"
   102	    git_hooks = basedir / ".git" / "hooks"
   103	
   104	    git_hooks.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   105	    for hook in hooks.iterdir():
   106	        dst = git_hooks / hook.name
   107	        if dst.exists():
   108	            if filecmp.cmp(hook, dst, shallow=False):
   109	                print(f"{hook.name} already installed.")
   110	                continue
   111	            raise RuntimeError(f"{dst} already exists; please remove it first")
   112	        else:
   113	            dst.symlink_to(hook)
   114	            print(f"{hook.name} installed at {dst}.")
   115	
   116	def build(dir: str, jobs: Optional[int], ninja: bool, unittest: bool, compiler: str, cmake_path: str, D: List[str],
   117	          skip_build: bool) -> None:
   118	    basedir = Path(__file__).parent.absolute()
   119	
   120	    find_command("autoconf", msg="autoconf is required to build jemalloc")
   121	    cmake = find_command(cmake_path, msg="CMake is required")
   122	
   123	    output = run_pipe(cmake, "-version")
   124	    output = run_pipe("head", "-n", "1", stdin=output)
   125	    output = run_pipe("awk", "{print $(NF)}", stdin=output)
   126	    cmake_version = output.read().strip()
   127	    check_version(cmake_version, CMAKE_REQUIRE_VERSION, "CMake")
   128	
   129	    os.makedirs(dir, exist_ok=True)
   130	
   131	    cmake_options = ["-DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=RelWithDebInfo"]
   132	    if ninja:
   133	        cmake_options.append("-G Ninja")
   134	    if compiler == 'gcc':
   135	        cmake_options += ["-DCMAKE_C_COMPILER=gcc", "-DCMAKE_CXX_COMPILER=g++"]
   136	    elif compiler == 'clang':
   137	        cmake_options += ["-DCMAKE_C_COMPILER=clang", "-DCMAKE_CXX_COMPILER=clang++"]
   138	    if D:
   139	        cmake_options += [f"-D{o}" for o in D]
   140	
   141	    run(cmake, str(basedir), *cmake_options, verbose=True, cwd=dir)
   142	
   143	    if skip_build:
   144	        return
   145	
   146	    target = ["kvrocks", "kvrocks2redis"]
   147	    if unittest:
   148	        target.append("unittest")
   149	
   150	    options = ["--build", "."]
   151	    if jobs is not None:
   152	        options.append(f"-j{jobs}")
   153	    options += ["-t", *target]
   154	
   155	    run(cmake, *options, verbose=True, cwd=dir)
   156	
   157	
   158	def get_source_files(dir: Path) -> List[str]:
   159	    return [
   160	        *glob(str(dir / "src/**/*.h"), recursive=True),
   161	        *glob(str(dir / "src/**/*.cc"), recursive=True),
   162	        *glob(str(dir / "tests/cppunit/**/*.h"), recursive=True),
   163	        *glob(str(dir / "tests/cppunit/**/*.cc"), recursive=True),
   164	        *glob(str(dir / "utils/kvrocks2redis/**/*.h"), recursive=True),
   165	        *glob(str(dir / "utils/kvrocks2redis/**/*.cc"), recursive=True),
   166	    ]
   167	
   168	
   169	def clang_format(clang_format_path: str, fix: bool = False) -> None:
   170	    command = find_command(clang_format_path, msg="clang-format is required")
   171	
   172	    version_res = run_pipe(command, '--version').read().strip()
   173	    version_re_res = re.search(r'version\s+((?:\w|\.)+)', version_res)
   174	    if version_re_res:
   175	        version_str = version_re_res.group(1)
   176	    else:
   177	        raise RuntimeError(f"version not found in `{command} --version`")
   178	
   179	    check_version(version_str, CLANG_FORMAT_REQUIRED_VERSION, "clang-format")
   180	
   181	    basedir = Path(__file__).parent.absolute()
   182	    sources = get_source_files(basedir)
   183	
   184	    if fix:
   185	        options = ['-i']
   186	    else:
   187	        options = ['--dry-run', '--Werror']
   188	
   189	    run(command, *options, *sources, verbose=True, cwd=basedir)
   190	
   191	
   192	def clang_tidy(dir: str, jobs: Optional[int], clang_tidy_path: str, run_clang_tidy_path: str, fix: bool) -> None:
   193	    # use the run-clang-tidy Python script provided by LLVM Clang
   194	    run_command = find_command(run_clang_tidy_path, msg="run-clang-tidy is required")
   195	    tidy_command = find_command(clang_tidy_path, msg="clang-tidy is required")
   196	
   197	    version_res = run_pipe(tidy_command, '--version').read().strip()
   198	    version_re_res = re.search(r'version\s+((?:\w|\.)+)', version_res)
   199	    if version_re_res:
   200	        version_str = version_re_res.group(1)
   201	    else:
   202	        raise RuntimeError(f"version not found in `{tidy_command} --version`")
   203	
   204	    check_version(version_str, CLANG_TIDY_REQUIRED_VERSION, "clang-tidy")
   205	
   206	    if not (Path(dir) / 'compile_commands.json').exists():
   207	        raise RuntimeError(f"expect compile_commands.json in build directory {dir}")
   208	
   209	    basedir = Path(__file__).parent.absolute()
   210	
   211	    options = ['-p', dir, '-clang-tidy-binary', tidy_command]
   212	    if jobs is not None:
   213	        options.append(f'-j{jobs}')
   214	
   215	    options.extend(['-fix'] if fix else [])
   216	
   217	    regexes = ['kvrocks/src/', 'utils/kvrocks2redis/', 'tests/cppunit/']
   218	
   219	    options.append(f'-header-filter={"|".join(regexes)}')
   220	
   221	    run(run_command, *options, *regexes, verbose=True, cwd=basedir)
   222	
   223	
   224	def golangci_lint(golangci_lint_path: str) -> None:
   225	    def get_gopath() -> Tuple[Path, Path]:
   226	        go = find_command('go', msg='go is required for testing')
   227	        gopath = run_pipe(go, 'env', 'GOPATH').read().strip()
   228	        bindir = Path(gopath).absolute() / 'bin'
   229	        binpath = bindir / 'golangci-lint'
   230	        return bindir, binpath
   231	
   232	    def get_syspath(sys_path: str) -> Tuple[str, str]:
   233	        golangci_command = find_command(sys_path, msg="golangci-lint is required")
   234	        version_res = run_pipe(golangci_command, '--version').read().strip()
   235	        version_re_res = re.search(r'version\s+((?:\w|\.)+)', version_res)
   236	        if version_re_res:
   237	            version_str = version_re_res.group(1)
   238	        else:
   239	            raise RuntimeError(f"version not found in `{golangci_command} --version`")
   240	        return golangci_command, version_str
   241	
   242	    def download_package(bindir: str) -> None:
   243	        output = run_pipe('curl', '-sfL', 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/golangci/golangci-lint/master/install.sh',
   244	                            verbose=True)
   245	        version_str = 'v' + '.'.join(map(str, GOLANGCI_LINT_REQUIRED_VERSION))
   246	        run('sh', '-s', '--', '-b', bindir, version_str, verbose=True, stdin=output)
   247	
   248	    if which(golangci_lint_path) is None:
   249	        bindir, binpath = get_gopath()
   250	        binpath_str = str(binpath)
   251	        if not binpath.exists():
   252	            download_package(str(bindir))
   253	
   254	    else:
   255	        binpath_str, version_str = get_syspath(golangci_lint_path)
   256	        check_version(version_str, GOLANGCI_LINT_REQUIRED_VERSION, "golangci-lint")
   257	
   258	    basedir = Path(__file__).parent.absolute() / 'tests' / 'gocase'
   259	    run(binpath_str, 'run', '-v', './...', cwd=str(basedir), verbose=True)
   260	
   261	
   262	def write_version(release_version: str) -> str:
   263	    version = release_version.strip()
   264	    if SEMVER_REGEX.match(version) is None:
   265	        raise RuntimeError(f"Kvrocks version should follow semver spec, got: {version}")
   266	
   267	    with open('src/VERSION.txt', 'w+') as f:
   268	        f.write(version)
   269	
   270	    return version
   271	
   272	
   273	def package_source(release_version: str, release_candidate_number: Optional[int]) -> None:
   274	    # 0. Write input version to VERSION file
   275	    version = write_version(release_version)
   276	
   277	    # 1. Git commit and tag
   278	    git = find_command('git', msg='git is required for source packaging')
   279	    run(git, 'commit', '-a', '-m', f'release: prepare source release apache-kvrocks-{version}')
   280	    if release_candidate_number is None:
   281	        run(git, 'tag', '-a', f'v{version}', '-m', f'release: copy for tag v{version}')
   282	    else:
   283	        run(git, 'tag', '-a', f'v{version}-rc{release_candidate_number}', '-m', f'release: copy for tag v{version}-rc{release_candidate_number}')
   284	
   285	    # 2. Create the source tarball
   286	    folder = f'apache-kvrocks-{version}-src'
   287	    tarball = f'apache-kvrocks-{version}-src.tar.gz'
   288	    run(git, 'archive', '--format=tar.gz', f'--output={tarball}', f'--prefix={folder}/', 'HEAD')
   289	
   290	    # 3. GPG Sign
   291	    gpg = find_command('gpg', msg='gpg is required for source packaging')
   292	    run(gpg, '--detach-sign', '--armor', tarball)
   293	
   294	    # 4. Generate sha512 checksum
   295	    shasum = find_command('shasum', msg='shasum is required for source packaging')
   296	    with open(f'{tarball}.sha512', 'w+') as f:
   297	        run(shasum, '-a', '512', tarball, stdout=f)
   298	
   299

   137	bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
   138	                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
   139	  // Parse the search key to extract namespace, type, and original key
   140	  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
   141	  const auto cf_handles = stor_->GetCFHandles();
   142	  
   143	  // storage closed would delete the column family handler and DB
   144	  if (!db || cf_handles->size() < 2) return false;
   145	
   146	  Slice input = key;
   147	  
   148	  // Extract namespace (1 byte size + data)
   149	  uint8_t ns_size = 0;
   150	  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_size)) return false;
   151	  if (input.size() < ns_size) return false;
   152	  
   153	  std::string ns(input.data(), ns_size);
   154	  input.remove_prefix(ns_size);
   155	  
   156	  // Extract type (1 byte)
   157	  uint8_t type_byte = 0;
   158	  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_byte)) return false;
   159	  
   160	  auto type = static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_byte);
   161	  
   162	  // Extract index name (4 bytes size + data)
   163	  Slice index_name;
   164	  if (!GetSizedString(&input, &index_name)) return false;
   165	  
   166	  // Handle different search subkey types
   167	  switch (type) {
   168	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META:
   169	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::PREFIXES: {
   170	      // These are metadata entries, we check if the index still exists
   171	      // by checking if we can read the INDEX_META key
   172	      std::string index_meta_key;
   173	      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, std::string_view(index_name.data(), index_name.size()));
   174	      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
   175	      
   176	      std::string index_meta_value;
   177	      auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Search)],
   178	                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
   179	      
   180	      // If this is the INDEX_META key itself, keep it
   181	      if (type == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) {
   182	        return false;
   183	      }
   184	      
   185	      // For PREFIXES, delete if INDEX_META doesn't exist
   186	      return s.IsNotFound();
   187	    }
   188	    
   189	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_META: {
   190	      // Field metadata - check if index exists
   191	      std::string index_meta_key;
   192	      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, std::string_view(index_name.data(), index_name.size()));
   193	      index_meta_key = search_key.ConstructIndexMeta();
   194	      
   195	      std::string index_meta_value;
   196	      auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Search)],
   197	                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
   198	      
   199	      return s.IsNotFound();
   200	    }
   201	    
   202	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD: {
   203	      // Field data - extract the field name
   204	      Slice field_name;
   205	      if (!GetSizedString(&input, &field_name)) return false;
   206	      
   207	      // The remaining part contains field-specific data and the original key
   208	      // For tag fields: tag (sized string) + key (sized string)
   209	      // For numeric fields: number (8 bytes) + key (sized string)
   210	      // For vector/hnsw fields: level (2 bytes) + level_type (1 byte) + key (sized string)
   211	      
   212	      Slice potential_key;
   213	      if (input.size() >= 4) {
   214	        // Try to parse as tag field (tag + key)
   215	        Slice tag;
   216	        Slice remaining = input;
   217	        if (GetSizedString(&remaining, &tag) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   218	          // Successfully parsed as tag field
   219	        } else {
   220	          // Try to parse as numeric field (double + key)
   221	          remaining = input;
   222	          double num;
   223	          if (GetDouble(&remaining, &num) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   224	            // Successfully parsed as numeric field
   225	          } else {
   226	            // Try to parse as hnsw field
   227	            // Structure: level (2 bytes) + level_type (1 byte) + key(s)
   228	            remaining = input;
   229	            uint16_t level;
   230	            uint8_t level_type;
   231	            if (input.size() >= 3 && GetFixed16(&remaining, &level) && GetFixed8(&remaining, &level_type)) {
   232	              // Check the level type
   233	              if (level_type == static_cast<uint8_t>(redis::HnswLevelType::NODE)) {
   234	                // HNSW node: just one key
   235	                if (!GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   236	                  // Could not parse, keep it to be safe
   237	                  return false;
   238	                }
   239	              } else if (level_type == static_cast<uint8_t>(redis::HnswLevelType::EDGE)) {
   240	                // HNSW edge: two keys (we'll check the first one)
   241	                if (!GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   242	                  // Could not parse, keep it to be safe
   243	                  return false;
   244	                }
   245	              } else {
   246	                // Unknown level type, keep it to be safe
   247	                return false;
   248	              }
   249	            } else {
   250	              // Could not parse any known field type, keep it to be safe
   251	              return false;
   252	            }
   253	          }
   254	        }
   255	        
   256	        // Now check if the original key exists and is not expired
   257	        std::string metadata_key = ComposeNamespaceKey(ns, potential_key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
   258	        std::string metadata_bytes;
   259	        auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Metadata)],
   260	                         metadata_key, &metadata_bytes);
   261	        
   262	        if (s.IsNotFound()) {
   263	          // Original key doesn't exist, delete this search entry
   264	          return true;
   265	        }
   266	        
   267	        if (!s.ok()) {
   268	          // Error reading metadata, keep the entry to be safe
   269	          return false;
   270	        }
   271	        
   272	        // Check if the key is expired
   273	        Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
   274	        rocksdb::Status decode_status = metadata.Decode(metadata_bytes);
   275	        if (!decode_status.ok()) {
   276	          // Failed to decode metadata, keep the entry to be safe
   277	          return false;
   278	        }
   279	        
   280	        // Delete if expired
   281	        return metadata.Expired();
   282	      }
   283	      
   284	      // Could not parse the key structure, keep it to be safe
   285	      return false;
   286	    }
   287	    
   288	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_ALIAS: {
   289	      // Field aliases - check if index exists
   290	      std::string index_meta_key;
   291	      redis::SearchKey search_key(ns, std::string_view(index_name.data(), index_name.size()));

   296	                       index_meta_key, &index_meta_value);
   297	      
   298	      return s.IsNotFound();
   299	    }

package search

import (
	"bytes"
	"context"
	"encoding/binary"
	"testing"

	"github.com/apache/kvrocks/tests/gocase/util"
	"github.com/redis/go-redis/v9"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
)

func SetBinaryBuffer(buf *bytes.Buffer, vec []float64) error {
	buf.Reset()

	for _, v := range vec {
		if err := binary.Write(buf, binary.LittleEndian, v); err != nil {
			return err
		}
	}

	return nil
}

func TestSearch(t *testing.T) {
	srv := util.StartServer(t, map[string]string{})
	defer srv.Close()

	ctx := context.Background()
	rdb := srv.NewClient()
	defer func() { require.NoError(t, rdb.Close()) }()

	t.Run("FT.CREATE", func(t *testing.T) {
		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "FT.CREATE", "testidx1", "ON", "JSON", "PREFIX", "1", "test1:", "SCHEMA", "a", "TAG", "b", "NUMERIC",
			"c", "VECTOR", "HNSW", "6", "TYPE", "FLOAT64", "DIM", "3", "DISTANCE_METRIC", "L2").Err())

		verify := func(t *testing.T) {
			require.Equal(t, []interface{}{"testidx1"}, rdb.Do(ctx, "FT._LIST").Val())
			infoRes := rdb.Do(ctx, "FT.INFO", "testidx1")
			require.NoError(t, infoRes.Err())
			idxInfo := infoRes.Val().([]interface{})
			require.Equal(t, "index_name", idxInfo[0])
			require.Equal(t, "testidx1", idxInfo[1])
			require.Equal(t, "index_definition", idxInfo[2])
			require.Equal(t, []interface{}{"key_type", "ReJSON-RL", "prefixes", []interface{}{"test1:"}}, idxInfo[3])
			require.Equal(t, "fields", idxInfo[4])
			require.Equal(t, []interface{}{"identifier", "a", "type", "tag", "properties", []interface{}{"separator", ",", "case_sensitive", false}}, idxInfo[5].([]interface{})[0])
			require.Equal(t, []interface{}{"identifier", "b", "type", "numeric", "properties", []interface{}{}}, idxInfo[5].([]interface{})[1])
			require.Equal(t, []interface{}{"identifier", "c", "type", "vector", "properties", []interface{}{"algorithm", "HNSW", "vector_type", "FLOAT64", "dim", int64(3), "distance_metric", "L2", "m", int64(16), "ef_construction", int64(200), "ef_runtime", int64(10), "epsilon", 0.01}}, idxInfo[5].([]interface{})[2])
		}
		verify(t)

		srv.Restart()
		verify(t)

		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "FT.CREATE", "testidx2", "SCHEMA", "x", "NUMERIC").Err())
		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "FT.DROPINDEX", "testidx2").Err())
	})

	t.Run("FT.SEARCH", func(t *testing.T) {
		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "JSON.SET", "test1:k1", "$", `{"a": "x,y", "b": 11, "c": [2,3,4]}`).Err())
		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "JSON.SET", "test1:k2", "$", `{"a": "x,z", "b": 22, "c": [12,13,14]}`).Err())
		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "JSON.SET", "test1:k3", "$", `{"a": "y,z", "b": 33, "c": [23,24,25]}`).Err())
		require.NoError(t, rdb.Do(ctx, "JSON.SET", "test2:k4", "$", `{"a": "x,y,z", "b": 44, "c": [33,34,35]}`).Err())

		verify := func(t *testing.T, res *redis.Cmd) {
			require.NoError(t, res.Err())
			require.Equal(t, 7, len(res.Val().([]interface{})))
			require.Equal(t, int64(3), res.Val().([]interface{})[0])
			require.Equal(t, "test1:k1", res.Val().([]interface{})[1])
			require.Equal(t, "test1:k2", res.Val().([]interface{})[3])
			require.Equal(t, "test1:k3", res.Val().([]interface{})[5])
		}

		res := rdb.Do(ctx, "FT.SEARCHSQL", "select * from testidx1")
		verify(t, res)
		res = rdb.Do(ctx, "FT.SEARCH", "testidx1", "*")
		verify(t, res)

		verify = func(t *testing.T, res *redis.Cmd) {

"""
Simple verification script to check that the SearchFilter implementation is correct
"""

import subprocess
import sys

def check_compilation():
    """Check that compact_filter.cc compiled successfully"""
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["ls", "-lah", "/testbed/build/CMakeFiles/kvrocks_objs.dir/src/storage/compact_filter.cc.o"],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True
    )
    if result.returncode != 0:
        print("ERROR: compact_filter.cc.o not found!")
        return False
    print("✓ compact_filter.cc compiled successfully")
    print(f"  {result.stdout.strip()}")
    return True

def check_code_structure():
    """Check that the code structure is correct"""
    with open("/testbed/src/storage/compact_filter.h", "r") as f:
        header_content = f.read()
    
    with open("/testbed/src/storage/compact_filter.cc", "r") as f:
        impl_content = f.read()
    
    checks = [
        ("SearchFilter class declaration", "class SearchFilter : public rocksdb::CompactionFilter" in header_content),
        ("SearchFilter constructor with storage", "explicit SearchFilter(Storage *storage)" in header_content),
        ("SearchFilterFactory with storage", "explicit SearchFilterFactory(engine::Storage *storage)" in header_content),
        ("SearchFilter::Filter implementation", "bool SearchFilter::Filter(" in impl_content),
        ("Namespace extraction", "GetFixed8(&input, &ns_size)" in impl_content),
        ("Type extraction", "static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_byte)" in impl_content),
        ("Handling INDEX_META", "case redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META:" in impl_content),
        ("Handling FIELD", "case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD:" in impl_content),
        ("Check for expired keys", "metadata.Expired()" in impl_content),
        ("Check for missing keys", "s.IsNotFound()" in impl_content),
        ("Storage passed to factory", "std::make_shared<SearchFilterFactory>(this)" in 
         open("/testbed/src/storage/storage.cc", "r").read()),
    ]
    
    all_passed = True
    for check_name, check_result in checks:
        if check_result:
            print(f"✓ {check_name}")
        else:
            print(f"✗ {check_name} FAILED")
            all_passed = False
    
    return all_passed

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Verifying SearchFilter implementation")
    print("=" * 60)
    print()
    
    if not check_compilation():
        return 1
    
    print()
    if not check_code_structure():
        return 1

    print("=" * 60)

    print("  * Entries referencing expired keys")
    print("  * Metadata entries for deleted indexes")
    
    return 0

    sys.exit(main())

   206	      
   207	      // The remaining part contains field-specific data and the original key
   208	      // For tag fields: tag (sized string) + key (sized string)
   209	      // For numeric fields: number (8 bytes) + key (sized string)
   210	      // For vector/hnsw fields: level (2 bytes) + level_type (1 byte) + key (sized string)
   211	      
   212	      Slice potential_key;
   213	      if (input.size() >= 4) {
   214	        // Try to parse as tag field (tag + key)
   215	        Slice tag;
   216	        Slice remaining = input;
   217	        if (GetSizedString(&remaining, &tag) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   218	          // Successfully parsed as tag field
   219	        } else {
   220	          // Try to parse as numeric field (double + key)
   221	          remaining = input;
   222	          double num;
   223	          if (GetDouble(&remaining, &num) && GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   224	            // Successfully parsed as numeric field
   225	          } else {
   226	            // Try to parse as hnsw field
   227	            // Structure: level (2 bytes) + level_type (1 byte) + key(s)
   228	            remaining = input;
   229	            uint16_t level;
   230	            uint8_t level_type;
   231	            if (input.size() >= 3 && GetFixed16(&remaining, &level) && GetFixed8(&remaining, &level_type)) {
   232	              // Check the level type
   233	              if (level_type == static_cast<uint8_t>(redis::HnswLevelType::NODE)) {
   234	                // HNSW node: just one key
   235	                if (!GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   236	                  // Could not parse, keep it to be safe
   237	                  return false;
   238	                }
   239	              } else if (level_type == static_cast<uint8_t>(redis::HnswLevelType::EDGE)) {
   240	                // HNSW edge: two keys (we'll check the first one)
   241	                if (!GetSizedString(&remaining, &potential_key)) {
   242	                  // Could not parse, keep it to be safe
   243	                  return false;
   244	                }
   245	              } else {
   246	                // Unknown level type, keep it to be safe
   247	                return false;
   248	              }
   249	            } else {
   250	              // Could not parse any known field type, keep it to be safe
   251	              return false;
   252	            }
   253	          }
   254	        }
   255	        
   256	        // Now check if the original key exists and is not expired
   257	        std::string metadata_key = ComposeNamespaceKey(ns, potential_key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
   258	        std::string metadata_bytes;
   259	        auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[static_cast<uint32_t>(ColumnFamilyID::Metadata)],
   260	                         metadata_key, &metadata_bytes);
   261	        
   262	        if (s.IsNotFound()) {
   263	          // Original key doesn't exist, delete this search entry
   264	          return true;
   265	        }
   266	        
   267	        if (!s.ok()) {
   268	          // Error reading metadata, keep the entry to be safe
   269	          return false;
   270	        }
   271	        
   272	        // Check if the key is expired
   273	        Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
   274	        rocksdb::Status decode_status = metadata.Decode(metadata_bytes);
   275	        if (!decode_status.ok()) {
   276	          // Failed to decode metadata, keep the entry to be safe
   277	          return false;
   278	        }
   279	        
   280	        // Delete if expired
   281	        return metadata.Expired();
   282	      }
   283	      
   284	      // Could not parse the key structure, keep it to be safe
   285	      return false;
   286	    }

   290	          // Failed to decode metadata, keep the entry to be safe
   291	          return false;
   292	        }
   293	        
   294	        // Delete if expired
   295	        return metadata.Expired();
   296	      }
   297	      
   298	      // Could not parse the key structure, keep it to be safe
   299	      return false;
   300	    }
   301	    
   302	    case redis::SearchSubkeyType::FIELD_ALIAS: {
   303	      // Field aliases - check if index exists
Review the changes and make sure they are as expected. Edit the file again if necessary.
